Located on Kingsland High Street, [[Mezcal]] Cantina is a fantastic small unpretentious authentic [[Mexican]] restaurant. Enjoy all the Mexican fare that Mezcal Cantina has to offer with authentic recipes for [[Salsa|salsa]], [[Stews|stews]], [[Tacos|tacos]], and more. Try their amazing Pozole.\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n}}\n====crepes====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 4 [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]]\n| 380 g [[La Costena Cuitlacoche]] (1 Cuitlacoche)\n| 6 chopped [[Mushrooms]] into slices\n| 3 [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Cloves|cloves]] finned chopped\n| 100g [[Jalapenos|jalapenos]] [[Chillies|chillies]]\n| 50g [[Onion|onion]] slices\n| 100g [[Sweet corn|sweet corn]]\n| [[Salt]] to taste\n}}\n====sauce====\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 100g [[Spinach|spinach]]\n| 50g [[Coriander|coriander]]\n| 100g [[Sour cream|sour cream]]\n| 4 [[Garlic|garlic]] [[Cloves|cloves]]\n| \u00bd [[Onion|onion]]\n| [[Salt]] to Taste\n}}\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n\n* preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n}}\n====first stage====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large pan place the [[Mushrooms|mushrooms]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Jalapeno chillies|jalapeno chillies]], [[Onions|onions]] & the [[Sweet corn|sweet corn]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 5-10 minutes.\n| Place [[La Costena Cuitlacoche]] into the pan on a low heat for about 20 minutes.\n}}\n====second stage====\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a pan, place the [[Garlic|garlic]] and the [[Onion|onion]] until they are [[Fried|fried]].\n| Put the [[Fried|fried]] [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Onion|onion]] into a [[Food processor|food processor]] and add the rest of the ingredients.\n| In a hot pan, warm the [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]].\n| Fill the [[Flour tortillas|flour tortillas]] with the [[Cuitlacoche]] (''Part 1'')\n| Add the [[Sauce|sauce]] on the top of the [[Flour tortilla|flour tortilla]] with a layer of [[Mozzarella cheese]].\n| Put into the [[Oven|oven]] for 3 minutes.\n| Serve with [[Rice|rice]] and La Costena refried pinto beans.\n}}\n==See also==\n\n* [[Cuitlacoche]] -                 "revisions": [

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Ensalada de coditos, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#ensaladadecoditos #coditos #tuna #cream #mayonnaise #tomatoes #pasta #egg #parsley #tomato #blackolives \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A simple pasta salad with tuna, tomatoes, egg, Cream and mayonnaise\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1529\n|PortionCalories = 382\n|DatePublished=9th March 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Ensalada de coditos recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Any pasta is fine</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.1</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">While a purist would say this has to be made with coditos, any pasta is fine in this salad.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n\n}}\n\nA simple [[Pasta salad|pasta salad]] with [[Tuna|tuna]], [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Egg|egg]], [[Cream|Cream]] and [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].   [[Coditos]] are generally used in Mexico, but the combination of the other ingredients is typically [[Spanish]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 300 g [[coditos]] (pasta) - see Variations below\n| 130g tin of [[Tuna|tuna]] in [[Oil|oil]], [[Mashed|mashed]]\n| [[Home-made mayonnaise|Mayonnaise]], using 500 ml [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n|  2 tablespoons of [[single cream]]\n| 500g firm [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], thinly sliced\n| A handful of [[Black olives|black olives]], pitted\n| 1 [[Egg|egg]], hard [[Boiled|boiled]], finely chopped or put through a [[Sieve|sieve]]\n| [[Parsley]], finely chopped\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Boil]] the [[coditos]] for about 15 minutes or per packet instructions.\n| Rinse under cold water and drain thoroughly.\n| When the [[Pasta|pasta]] is cold, mix with the [[Tuna|tuna]], [[Cream|Cream]] and [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]] and place in the middle of a serving dish.\n| Arrange the [[Tomato|tomato]] slices around the [[Pasta|pasta]] and place the [[Olives|olives]] on top of it.\n| Sprinkle with the [[Hard boiled egg|hard boiled egg]]. and the [[Parsley|parsley]].\n}}\n===Variations===\n[[Coditos]] are not available in the UK, as far I can ascertain, although it may be found as elbow macaroni.  They are similar in shape to the [[Italian]] [[:Image:Pasta 2006 3.jpg|pipe pasta]] and this type can be used instead.\n[[Elicoidali]] is another fairly close equivalent that can be purchased directly from Waitrose.\n\nI already had some [[homemade garlic mayonnaise]], but had no idea how much would be made from 500 ml of olive oil, however,  3 good tablespoons of mayonnaise seemed just fine.  I also garnished the salad with a little [[smoked paprika]] to add a bit of extra interest.\nMany people like to use [[Cream|Cream]] in this salad because it reduces acidity in the dish due to the [[Mayonnaise|mayonnaise]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Pasta recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Pasta salad recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes|Ensalada de coditos]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#ensaladadecoditos #coditos #tuna #cream #mayonnaise #tomatoes #pasta #egg #parsley #tomato #blackolives </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

less spicy version.\n| 3 [[Gluten|gluten]] green [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]\n| 1 cup [[Shredded|shredded]] [[Mozzarella|mozzarella cheese]]\n| 1 cup [[Goya Salsa Rojo Mexicana]]\n| 3 sprinkling a bit of [[Salt|salt]] for flavour, under low-medium heat until set and transfer to a plate.  Then divide the [[Eggs|eggs]] in half.\n| Combine [[Adobo|adobo]], [[Salsa Roja]], [[Cilantro paste]] and [[Green onion|green onion]].\n| Place [[Corn|corn]] [[Tortilla|tortilla]] on [[Skillet|skillet]]. title": "Gorditas recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Gorditas recipe Vegetarian, from Cookipedia.Co.Uk\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#masaharina #masa #tortilla #dough #yellowcornmeal #gorditas #bakingpowder #gorditasrecipe #vegetableoil #frying #flour \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A gordita in Mexican cuisine is a food which is characterised by a small, thick tortilla made with masa harina (processed corn flour)\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1225\n|PortionCalories = 204\n|DatePublished=31st January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|ImageComment = 11 very lazily rolled gorditas\n |Servings = Serves 6 - Makes 11 to 12 [[Gorditas|gorditas]]\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 25 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Gorditas rolled.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Corn tortillas</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These are lovely.  You must make them with Masa Harina, they won't be the same using normal cornmeal.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''A gordita''' in [[Mexican cuisine]] is a food which is characterised by a small, thick [[tortilla]] made with [[masa harina]] (processed corn flour). The gordita is in contrast to a [[taco]], which uses a thinner [[tortilla]]. \"Gordita\" means \"little fat one\" in Spanish. The gordita is typically baked on a comal, a small pan similar to a [[tava]].\n\nThe gordita's thick [[tortilla]] is typically split and filled with guisos (soups or stews) or casseroles, like [[chicken]], [[cochinita pibil]], [[nopales]], carne al pastor, etc. These are made mostly for lunch and are accompanied by many different types of [[salsas]]. The most traditional \"gordita\" in the central region of Mexico is filled with \"[[chicharr\u00f3n]] prensado\" (a type of stew made with pork rind and spices) and is called \"gordita de chicharr\u00f3n\".\nIn Durango, Mexico, gorditas are commonly made from wheat [[flour]] (harina de trigo) [[tortillas]] and look more like small [[pita breads]]. The [[dough]] (masa) is identical to that of the [[flour tortilla]]. It is cooked on a griddle (comal) with a hot piece of metal placed on top that resembles a clothes iron. The gordita fills up with steam and a small slit is cut into one side where it can be filled with guisados.\n\nThe best gorditas are made with [[Masa harina|masa harina]], though you can make them with [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] if you cannot obtain [[Masa harina|masa harina]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250g [[Masa harina|masa harina]] or fine [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]]\n| &#189; level teaspoon of [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 1 heaped teaspoon of [[Baking powder|baking powder]]\n| 350 ml very hot water\n| [[Yellow cornmeal]] for rolling\n| [[Vegetable oil]] for [[Frying|frying]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add the [[Masa|masa]] and [[Salt|salt]] to a large bowl and make a well in the centre.\n| Mix the [[Baking powder|baking powder]] into the hot water and pour into the centre of the [[Masa|masa]].\n| Using a spoon, fold the [[Masa|masa]] into the water, once it begins to combine, [[Kneading bread|knead]] with your hands until a firm malleable [[Dough|dough]] is produced.\n| Divide the [[Dough|dough]] into 12 balls, dust the work surface with cornmeal and roll each one out to about the size of a fried egg, leaving them quite thick.\n| Heat a large [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and add a few glugs of [[Oil|oil]]\n| Fill the pan with as many [[Gorditas|gorditas]] as will fit and [[Fry|fry]] for 3 minutes a side, turning once.  They are ready to eat once they have [[Puffed|puffed]] up a little.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nSlice them open like [[Pitta breads|pitta breads]] and fill with [[Mexican]] treats\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Ingredients]]\n[[Category:Prepared foods]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#masaharina #masa #tortilla #dough #yellowcornmeal #gorditas #bakingpowder #gorditasrecipe #vegetableoil #frying #flour </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }

The drink reputedly originated at Tujague's, a landmark bar in the [[French]] Quarter of New Orleans, Louisiana, and gained popularity during the 1950s and 1960s throughout the American South.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 30 ml (1 part) Cr\u00e8me de menthe (green)\n| 30 ml (1 part) Cr\u00e8me de [[Cacao|cacao]] (white)\n| 30 ml (1 part) Fresh [[Cream|cream]]\n}}\n\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Pour ingredients into a [[Cocktail shaker|cocktail shaker]] with ice. \n| Shake briskly and then strain into a chilled [[Cocktail glass|cocktail glass]].\n}}\n==See also==\n* [[Cuban Chocolate Grasshopper Pie]]\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes]]\n[[Category:Alcoholic beverages]]\n[[Category:Historic recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#drink #cocktailglass #cacao #grasshoppercocktail #cream #cocktailshaker #french #grasshopper #mint </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

small [[onion]], roughtly chopped\n| 2 peeled [[Garlic|garlic]] cloves\n| Handful  of [[coriander leaves]], chopped (or [[parsley]] at a push)\n| Juice of a [[lime]]\n| 3 fresh [[red chillies]]\n| [[Sea salt]] and [[freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| [[Avocado|Prepare the avocados]]: cut the [[avocados]] in half, remove the stones and scoop the flesh out with a tablespoon and place in a [[food processor]]\n| Add the [[lime juice]] to the [[avocados]] and blend until smooth\n| Add the remaining ingredients and blend until properly mixed\n| Cover and chill for 1 hour, then serve\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe chilled with [[tortilla chips]]\nYou can also serve it with fried plantains. \n===Variations===\n* add 4 tablespoons of [[sour cream]]\n* add a teaspoon of freshly ground [[cumin seeds]]\n==See also==\n{{GuacamoleRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#guacamolerecipe #avocados #tortillachips #sourcream #limejuice #foodprocessor #cuminseeds #parsley #tomatoes #garlic #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Guacamole rojo",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Guacamole rojo recipe Cooking with chillies\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#tomatoes #guacamolerojo #lime #garlic #lemonjuice #onion #guacamole #avocadooil #avocados #hassavocados #chillies \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=This is red guacamole, so called because of the large amount of tomatoes used in it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1174\n|PortionCalories = 293\n|DatePublished=20th October 2012\n|Author = JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 4 as an accompaniment\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = 15 minutes\n |CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Guacamole rojo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">See what you mean Julia</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.53</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This is a nice as a dip for pitta breads</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\nThis is red [[Guacamole|guacamole]], so called because of the large amount of [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] used in it.  Because of its coarse texture, it is more suited as an [[Accompaniment|accompaniment]] than a [[Dip|dip]].\n\nThe recipe has been translated and slightly adapted from Ricardo Mu\u00f1oz Zurita's book '''Salsas Mexicanas''' (ISBN 9702222125)\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 600g ripe [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], cut into 0.5cm cubes\n| &frac12; small [[Onion|onion]], finely chopped\n| [[Garlic]] to taste, finely chopped\n| 25g [[Coriander leaves|coriander leaves]], chopped\n| 3 [[Green chillies|green chillies]], finely chopped\n| 30ml [[Avocado oil|avocado oil]]\n| 3 medium, or 2 large [[hass avocados]]\n| [[Lime]] or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]]\n| [[Salt]], to taste\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Onion|onion]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Coriander|coriander]] and the [[Chillies|chillies]] in a bowl.\n| Cut the [[Avocados|avocados]] in half, remove the stone and using a spoon, extract all of the flesh.\n| With a fork, coarsely [[Mash|mash]] the flesh and mix with the remaining ingredients and the [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]].\n| Add [[Salt|salt]] to taste.\n}}\n==See also==\n{{GuacamoleRecipes}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Accompaniments]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#tomatoes #guacamolerojo #lime #garlic #lemonjuice #onion #guacamole #avocadooil #avocados #hassavocados #chillies </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Home-made Churros",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Home-made Churros, Spanish recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from potato dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 120\n|PortionCalories = 24\n|DatePublished=8th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 5\n|Difficulty = 2\n|ImageComment = Churros and chocolate\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Churros recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">One is enough!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">2</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">These are more unhealthy than deep-fried Mars Bars.  Yuk!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nA churro is a fried-dough pastry-based snack, sometimes made from [[potato]] dough, originated in Spain, and is popular in Latin America, France, Portugal, the USA, and Spanish-speaking Caribbean islands. It is sometimes referred to as a Spanish doughnut or Mexican doughnut. The snack gets its name from its shape, which resembles the horns of the Churro breed of sheep reared in the Spanish grasslands of Huarocho. There are two types of churros in Spain. One is long and fat and the other, specially popular in Madrid, is thin and knotted (porra). They both are normally eaten for breakfast dipped in hot chocolate (drink).\nThe churro is typically fried to a crunchy consistency and sometimes sprinkled with [[sugar]]. Its surface is ridged due to being piped from a [[churrera]], a syringe with a star-shaped nozzle.\n\nLike [[pretzels]], churros are often sold by street vendors who in many cases will fry them freshly on the street stand and sell them hot. In Spain and Mexico, they are available in cafes for breakfast, although they may be found throughout the day and night as a snack.\n\nVery popular for breakfast, churros are a simple type of doughnut.  They can be made with a [[churrera]], obtainable from [http://www.delicioso.co.uk/ Delicioso] and [[Orce Serrano Hams]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| Measuring in a [[cup or jug]], you need equal volumes of [[Plain flour|plain flour]] and water, so for this recipe measure 500 ml of both\n| Large pinch of [[Salt|salt]]\n| [[Olive]] or [[Sunflower oil|sunflower oil]]\n| Caster or [[Icing sugar|icing sugar]] (optional)\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Put the water and [[Salt|salt]] in a saucepan and bring to the [[Boil|boil]].\n| [[Sieve]] the [[Flour|flour]] into a bowl.\n| Add the [[Boiling|boiling]] water to the [[Flour|flour]] and mix thoroughly with a fork.  The mixture should be like a thick paste.\n| Do not worry too much about any lumps as the force on the churrera will disperse them.\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large [[Deep frying|deep frying]] or saut\u00e9 pan.\n| Force the mixture into the [[churrera]] as tightly as you can, to reduce the amount of air in the mixture.\n| When the [[Oil|oil]] is almost [[Smoking|smoking]], pipe the dough into the pan, either in a spiral or in longish strips.  \n| Cook until they are a rich golden [[Brown|brown]].  Because they float, you will need to turn them over to ensure even cooking.  This is best done with either [[skewers]] or chopsticks.\n| If they are spiral shaped, cut them into long pieces with scissors.\n| Sprinkle them with [[Sugar|sugar]] if desired\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Churros ready to be frozen.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Churros ready to be frozen\nImage:Cooked, frozen, home-made churros.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Home-made, frozen and cooked churros\n</gallery>\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe hot with a cup of thick dark drinking [[Chocolate|chocolate]] into which the churros are dunked.  Unless you have quite a sweet tooth, I would avoid sprinkling them with the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n\nThis recipe makes 10 large churros.  Allow 2-3 per person.\n\n===Variations===\nThe above is a very basic recipe and in my experience the more usual one.  However, sometimes [[Potatoes|potatoes]] and/or [[Eggs|eggs]] are included.\n\nAlthough they would lose their authenticity, you can play around with them and add any flavourings you like.  I have made them with [[Garlic|garlic]] and [[Paprika|paprika]] before.\n\n===Chef's tip===\nYou can use a [[deep fat fryer]] to cook the churros, but it is quite difficult to pipe in the mixture if your fryer is a long thin one.  They would probably work better in a round fryer.\n\nAs an alternative to a [[churrera]], it is possible to make them using a [[piping bag]] with a large star-shaped nozzle, although not quite so easy.\n\nChurros can be [[Frozen|frozen]].  Pipe them onto [[greaseproof paper]], or preferably [[Bake-O-Glide]] - it can be quite tricky extracting them from [[greaseproof paper]]. [[Open freeze]] them until they are hard (several hours), then put them into bags.  They should be cooked directly from [[frozen]].  If they are [[frozen]], they are easier to cook in a [[deep fat fryer]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking|Churros]]\n[[Category:Spanish recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Churros]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Churros]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Deep fried]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#churrera #frozen #homemadechurros #greaseproofpaper #deepfatfryer #flour #icingsugar #boiling #potato #orceserranohams #cuporjug </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Homemade tortilla chips, Vegetarian recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#corntortillas #homemadetortillachips #vegetableoil #chips #tortillachips #oliveoil #masaharina #panfried #corntortillarecipe #salsa #fry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Tortilla chips are made by shallow frying soft corn tortillas - these instructions just cover the frying part so can hardly be considered a recipe\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1342\n|PortionCalories = 671\n|DatePublished=23rd October 2012\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 15 minutes\n |PrepTime = None\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Homemade tortilla chips recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Love this.</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Brilliant idea.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]]</span></span>\n}}\n\n[[Tortilla chips]] are made by shallow [[Frying|frying]] soft [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] - these instructions just cover the frying part so can hardly be considered a recipe!\n\nIf you want to start from scratch, [[Corn tortilla recipe|use this recipe]] to make the soft corn tortillas yourself.  It's the [[masa harina]] that gives them that unique flavour.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| &#189; cup of [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 pack of soft [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]] (8 to 10 tortillas)\n| Fine [[Salt|salt]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Cut the each [[Corn tortillas|corn tortilla]] into 6 triangles\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a large heavy based [[Frying pan|frying pan]] over a medium heat.\n| Add the triangles in small batches and [[Fry|fry]] for about a minute or until they just start to [[Brown|brown]].  You need to be quick as they can burn easily.\n| Lift the cooked [[Chips|chips]] out of the pan and let the [[Oil|oil]] drain and then stack on paper towels to remove excess oil.\n| Sprinkle with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]].\n| Allow to cool and crisp-up a little before serving.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nTry one of our [[Salsa|salsa recipes]] or this [[Tex-Mex bean dip for tacos]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFor health reasons, I have used [[Olive oil|olive oil]].\n\nYou could possibly fry the whole tortilla first and then cut into triangles as they remain soft for a ref minutes after frying.  I will try that next time I make these.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Bread and baking]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cookery cheats]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#corntortillas #homemadetortillachips #vegetableoil #chips #tortillachips #oliveoil #masaharina #panfried #corntortillarecipe #salsa #fry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Hot cheese and tomato hummus",
                "revisions": [

                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Hot cheese and tomato hummus recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#hummus #dried #oliveoil #hotcheeseandtomatohummus #refrigerated #vegetablestock #bean #chillisauce #driedblacklentils #butterbeans #lockandlock \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=A spicy bean pur\u00e9e based on a Mexican bean and cheese puree\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1591\n|PortionCalories = 397\n|DatePublished=17th August 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 17 hours\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 4 hours 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Hot cheese and tomato hummus.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Dipalicious!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">The melted cheese on the top makes all the difference.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nNot really a [[hummus]], as I've not heard of a hot [[hummus]] before now. It's really a spicy [[bean]] [[pur\u00e9e]].  It's based on a [[Mexican bean and cheese puree]] and made with leftovers from the [[freezer]].  I added the sliced tomatoes to prevent the bean [[pur\u00e9e]] from drying out.\n\nA fantastic recipe and you would never imagine it was [[vegetarian]]!\n\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 90 g [[Dried|dried]] [[haricot beans]]\n| 90 g [[Dried|dried]] [[butter beans]]\n| 2 [[Litres|litres]] of weak [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]] - I make up half the advised quantity of [[Bouillon|bouillon]] powder.\n| 2 sticks of [[celery]], roughly chopped\n| 1 large [[sweet pepper]], deseeded and chopped\n| 1 bulb of [[garlic]], peeled and crushed (''or to taste'')\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and roughly chopped\n| 3 tablespoons [[olive oil]]\n| 1 tablespoon of [[Tex-Mex seasoning]], or [[Old India Taco Seasoning]], or chopped [[chillies]], or [[chilli sauce]].\n| 110 g mature [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], roughly [[Grated|grated]].\n| 3 large tomatoes, thinly sliced\n| 1 to 2 tablespoons of yellow cornmeal.  Use '''only''' if the mixture looks far too wet and the end of the slow cooking process.\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n*  When you are ready to start the final bake, preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the beans in cold water overnight, rinsing and draining a few times if possible.\n| Add the soaked beans, stock, celery, peppers, garlic, chopped onion, Tex-Mex seasoning (or equivalent) to a [[slow cooker]] on low and cook for 4 hours\n| Using a [[stick blender]] reduce the mixture to the consistency of [[hummus]].  If it is really wet, add a tablespoon of [[yellow cornmeal]], stir well and check in another 15 minutes.  This is a very efficient way of reducing liquid, but use with caution as more than once, I've had to add more stock after doing this!\n| Add 1.5 tablespoons of olive oil.  Mix well and remove from the heat.\n| At this stage the mixture could be [[refrigerated]] or even [[frozen]] and the final cooking stage done at a later time.\n| Once the [[Oven|oven]] is hot, coat a [[shallow oven proof dish]] with 1.5 tablespoons of olive oil and spread the bean mixture evenly over the surface.\n| Sprinkle with grated [[cheese]] and top with the thinly sliced tomatoes.\n| [[Bake|bake]] the [[Puree|puree]] for about 45 minutes to 1 hour.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[soured cream]] and plain [[tortilla chips]] or broken up [[taco shells]] to use as edible spoons!\n\nThis dish is equally good hot or cold.  Store any unused [[pur\u00e9e]] in a [[Lock and Lock]] style box to prevent it drying out.\n===Chef's notes===\nI used [[dried black lentils]] for the beans and for health reasons, [[olive oil]] for the vegetable oil as this recipe uses rather a lot. For the cheese I used a mixture of mature [[gouda]] and mature [[cheddar]].\n\n===Variations===\nThis is a great recipe for experimentation.  Almost any vegetables can be added to this recipe.  Just use your imagination!\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#hummus #dried #oliveoil #hotcheeseandtomatohummus #refrigerated #vegetablestock #bean #chillisauce #driedblacklentils #butterbeans #lockandlock </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Huevos Rancheros",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Huevos Rancheros, Egg recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#huevosrancheros #eggs #tomatoes #tortillas #fry #simmer #chilipowder #onion #sauce #parsley #garlic \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Huevos Rancheros (Spanish for \"eggs ranch-style\") is a traditional Mexican country breakfast\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1137\n|PortionCalories = 568\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 20 minutes\n|PrepTime = 5 minutes\n|CookTime = 15 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Huevos Rancheros recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Breakfast eggs!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Nice and spicy - I love these with freshly squeezed orange juice.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\n'''Huevos Rancheros''' (Spanish for \"[[Eggs|eggs]] ranch-style\") is a traditional [[Mexican]] country breakfast. From its home in Mexico, the dish has spread throughout the Americas.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 3 tablespoons (45ml) [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 medium [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 1 [[Clove|clove]] [[Garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| A pinch [[Chili powder|chili powder]]\n| 4 [[Plum|plum]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], peeled, seeded and chopped\n| 2 [[Corn tortillas|corn tortillas]]\n| 2 [[free range eggs]]\n| Chopped [[Chilli peppers|chilli peppers]], to taste\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]], to taste\n| 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Coriander|coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| To prepare the ranchero sauce, in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]], heat 1 tablespoon [[Oil|oil]] over medium heat\n| Add the [[Onion|onion]] and [[Garlic|garlic]], and saut\u00e9 until softened, 4 or 5 minutes\n| Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Peppers|peppers]], [[Chili powder|chili powder]], [[Salt|salt]] and a few grinds of [[Black pepper|black pepper]] and reduce to a [[Simmer|simmer]]\n| [[Simmer]] for about 10 minutes, until the [[Sauce|sauce]] begins to thicken\n| Add the [[Coriander|coriander]] or [[Parsley|parsley]], turn off the heat and cover the pan to keep the [[Sauce|sauce]] warm\n| In another [[Frying pan|frying pan]], lightly [[Fry|fry]] the [[Tortillas|tortillas]] in 1 tablespoon of [[Oil|oil]]. Remove and drain\n| If necessary, add additional [[Oil|oil]] to the second [[Frying pan|frying pan]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Eggs|eggs]] until they are \"[[How to fry an egg|sunny-side up]]\". \n| Transfer the [[Eggs|eggs]] to the [[Tortillas|tortillas]], and cover with the ranchero sauce\n| Serve immediately\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Egg recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Breakfast recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#huevosrancheros #eggs #tomatoes #tortillas #fry #simmer #chilipowder #onion #sauce #parsley #garlic </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie a beef recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#insideoutmeatandchillibeanpie #foodprocessor #oliveoil #frenchstick #beans #parsley #passata #mexican #sirloinsteak #jarlsbergcheese #pastry \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Time for another experiment! The pie is formed inside-out - the meat being the 'pastry' and the spicy beans being the filling. The ingredients I have\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3188\n|PortionCalories = 531\n|DatePublished=24th October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = The inside of an inside-out meat pie\n |Servings = Serves 6 to 8 people with side dishes\n |Difficulty = 3\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 40 minutes\n |PrepTime = 40 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour\n |Image = [[Image:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wierd!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Still tasted like a 'right-way around' meat pie.</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nTime for another experiment!\n\nThe pie is formed inside-out - the [[Meat|meat]] being the '[[Pastry|pastry]]' and the spicy [[Beans|beans]] being the filling.\n\nThe ingredients I have chosen to use have no specific geographical origin, I just felt that they would go well together in this.   Use what you have that is similar.\n\n''Based on 'Marc Garcy's savoury pie' from the [[Mexican]] cook-book: 'Two Cooks and a Suitcase' - Doug Bell & Rhoda Robertson -  a great book that unfortunately falls apart when you try and read it.''\n\n'''A [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade is helpful when making this recipe'''\n\n'''''pie pastry'''''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 200 ml [[Passata|passata]]\n| 450 g [[Minced|minced]] [[sirloin steak]] - I blitzed the cubed steak in a [[food processor]] for a minute to mince it.\n| 1 [[Onion|onion]], peeled and finely chopped\n| 2 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] peeled and crushed\n| 1 green [[Sweet pepper|sweet pepper]], deseeded and finely chopped\n| 1/4 of a [[French stick]] blitzed to breadcrumbs in a [[food processor]]\n| 1 beaten [[Egg|egg]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Smoked paprika|smoked paprika]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''''pie filling'''''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 400g can [[Red kidney beans|red kidney beans]], rinsed well & drained\n| 200 ml [[Passata|passata]]\n| 2 cups cooked [[Basmati rice|basmati rice]] - (from just less than 1 cup of uncooked [[rice]].\n| 1 tablespoon [[Curry paste|curry paste]] - or whatever you fancy to add a little bite\n| 1/2 a teaspoon of Mexican oregano\n| 3 tablespoons of [[olive oil]]\n| Splash of [[red wine]] or [[vinegar]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''''topping'''''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| &#188; [[French stick]] blitzed to breadcrumbs in a [[food processor]]\n| 100g g [[Grated|grated]] [[Jarlsberg cheese]] - nicer and way cheaper than [[Emmenthal]]\n| [[Olive oil]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''''garnish'''''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| Fresh [[Parsley|parsley]], chopped finely\n\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour]\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie out of oven.jpg|Fresh out of the oven\nImage:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie oven ready.jpg|Ready for the oven\nImage:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie lined and filled.jpg|The pie dish (casserole dish) lined and filled\nImage:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie lined.jpg|The pie dish (casserole dish) lined with the meat 'pastry\nImage:Inside-out meat and chilli bean pie ingredients.jpg|The ingredients\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n'''''the crust'''''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Turn the [[French stick]] into [[Breadcrumbs|breadcrumbs]] - don't forget to save some for the topping.\n| I use fresh [[Bread|bread]], roughly sliced. Add to a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and blitz into crumbs.\n| Add all of the crust ingredients to a bowl and mix well with your hands.\n| Lightly [[Spray|spray]] or grease a [[Pie dish|pie dish]] and line it with the [[Meat|meat]] - You'll need a big dish - I used a Pyrex casserole dish\n'''''the filling'''''\n| Add the rinsed [[Beans|beans]] to a bowl and roughly crush them with the end of a [[Rolling pin|rolling pin]]\n| Add the remaining ingredients and mix well with your hands\n| Add the filling to the pie\n}}\n'''''the topping'''''\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Mix all of the topping ingredients together and sprinkle over the top\n| Drizzle with a little [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| Cover with [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] and [[Bake|bake]] for 1 hour\n| Remove the [[Tin-foil|tin-foil]] for the last 15  minutes\n| Sprinkle with freshly chopped [[parsley]] and serve\n}}\n===Chef's notes===\nThis was very tasty dish.  It could have done with more gravy and maybe a thinner meat 'pastry'.  A great starting point for further ideas none-the-less.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Rice recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#insideoutmeatandchillibeanpie #foodprocessor #oliveoil #frenchstick #beans #parsley #passata #mexican #sirloinsteak #jarlsbergcheese #pastry </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Margarita recipe",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Margarita recipe Cocktail, from Cookipedia.Co.Uk\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#margaritarecipe #tequila #lime #frozen #limejuice #triplesec #lemonjuice #dip \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=The margarita is a cocktail consisting of tequila mixed with triple sec and lime or lemon juice, often served with salt on the glass rim\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 744\n|PortionCalories = 372\n|DatePublished=21st August 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 1\n |Difficulty = 1\n |TotalTime = 5 minutes\n |PrepTime = 5 minutes \n |CookTime = None\n |Image = [[Image:Margarita recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">mmm, salty!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Don't normally like cocktail, but I like these</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Klapaucius|Klapaucius]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nThe margarita is a cocktail consisting of [[Tequila|tequila]] mixed with triple sec and [[Lime|lime]] or [[Lemon juice|lemon juice]], often served with [[Salt|salt]] on the glass rim.  The drink is usually served shaken with ice, on the rocks, blended with ice ([[Frozen|frozen]] margarita) or without ice (straight up). All three methods are frequently served with salt or [[Sugar|sugar]] on the rim of the glass which is optional.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 2 parts [[Tequila]]\n| 1 part [[Triple sec]]\n| 1 part freshly squeezed [[Lime juice|lime juice]]\n| Ice cubes for chilling\n| Fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] for the rim of the glass (optional)\n| Thinly slices of lime to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Rub a wedge of [[Lime|lime]] around the rim of the glass and then [[Dip|dip]] in fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| Mix the remaining ingredients in a cocktail shaker or jug\n| Strain into glasses, leaving the ice behind so as not to dilute the cocktail\n| Garnish with a slice of lime\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Drink and beverage recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#margaritarecipe #tequila #lime #frozen #limejuice #triplesec #lemonjuice #dip </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Mexican bean and cheese puree",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mexican bean and cheese puree a cheese recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#beans #mexicanbeanandcheesepuree #oliveoil #simmer #grated #bean #stock #chillies #tabascosauce #mexican #mexico \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Based on a recipe from my cookbook of the moment: Diana Kennedy's wonderful Mexican cookbook, Essential cuisines of Mexico\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2347\n|PortionCalories = 586\n|DatePublished=20th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 4 to 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 15 hours\n |PrepTime = 12 hours 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 2 hours 45 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mexican bean and cheese puree recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"><span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Wow! I remember this</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">This was great and it's veggie!</span> \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\">[[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\n{{Template:AdvancePreparationIcon}}\n\nBased on a recipe from my cookbook of the moment: Diana Kennedy's wonderful [[Mexican]] cookbook, ''Essential cuisines of [[Mexico]]'' ISBN 9780307587725, this Mexican baked bean recipe would make a great side dish, a snack-style lunch dip for crispy tortilla chips or even a main course.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 180 g [[Dried|dried]] [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]]\n| 2 [[Litres|litres]] of weak [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n| &#189; a small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and roughly chopped\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 100 ml [[olive oil]]\n| 1/2 to 1 teaspoon [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 110 ml full [[Cream|cream]] [[Milk|milk]]\n| 3 [[Ancho chillies|ancho chillies]], rehydrated and deseeded\n| 110 g strong [[Cheddar cheese|cheddar cheese]], roughly [[Grated|grated]].\n| Freshly ground [[black pepper]] and [[Tabasco sauce]] to taste\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n*  Preheat the [[Oven|oven]] to 180\u00b0 C (350\u00b0 F - gas 4), [fan oven 160\u00b0 C & reduce cooking time by 10 mins per hour].\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Soak the beans in cold water overnight, rinsing and draining a few times if possible.\n| Cover the beans with twice the volume of cold water, bring to the boil and simmer uncovered for 30 minutes.  Skim any scum that appears on the surface.\n| Drain the beans and return to the pan. Pour 1.5 tablespoons of [[Oil|oil]] over the beans, add the onion pieces and the stock. Bring to the boil, cover and reduce to a simmer.\n| [[Simmer]] for about 30 minutes or until they are softening and the skins beginning to [[Split|split]].\n| Add the 100 ml of olive oil to a [[Casserole dish|casserole dish]] and place in the oven whilst it is preheating.\n| Add the [[Salt|salt]] and continue to [[Simmer|simmer]] for another 35 minutes until the [[Beans|beans]] become a mush.  this time will very depending upon the type of bean.\n| If they dry out during this stage add a little more [[Stock|stock]].\n| Remove the [[Beans|beans]] from the heat, drain them and using a [[Food processor|food processor]], blend them to a pur\u00e9e with the [[Milk|milk]] and [[chillies]].\n| Taste for seasoning and add [[Tabasco sauce]] to taste if using.\n| Once the [[Oven|oven]] is hot, carefully stir the [[Bean|bean]] pur\u00e9e into the hot [[Oil|oil]] and mix very well.  Don't be concerned about the obvious amount of excess oil, this will absorb into the bean mixture during the last 15 minutes of cooking. \n| Return the [[Casserole|casserole]] of [[Beans|beans]] to the [[Oven|oven]] and [[Bake|bake]] the [[Puree|puree]] for about 45 minutes to 1 hour.\n| By now the [[Beans|beans]] should be [[Drying|drying]] out at the edges, don't add any more [[Stock|stock]] at this stage.\n| Sprinkle the [[Beans|beans]] with the [[Grated|grated]] [[Cheese|cheese]] and return to the [[Oven|oven]] for 15 minutes or until melted.\n| Serve directly.\n}}\n===Variations===\nI like to fiddle with my recipes and encouraged by the recent success [[Dal makhani]], I also added 3 fat crushed cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] and 200 ml of chopped tomatoes at the blending stage.\n\n[[Dried|dried]] [[Kidney beans|kidney beans]], [[chick peas]] or any similar dried [[Bean|bean]] work fine in this recipe.\n\nI think that [[yogurt]] would work just as well as [[milk]] too.\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with [[soured cream]] and plain [[tortilla chips]] to use as edible spoons!\n===Chef's notes===\nI used [[dried black lentils]] for the beans and for health reasons, [[olive oil]] for the vegetable oil as this recipe uses rather a lot. For the cheese I used a mixture of mature [[gouda]] and mature [[cheddar]].\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Grain and bean recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetable recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Baked or roasted]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#beans #mexicanbeanandcheesepuree #oliveoil #simmer #grated #bean #stock #chillies #tabascosauce #mexican #mexico </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[The Cool Chile co]] can supply these.\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 tablespoon [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 1 cup, 250 ml raw unsalted shelled [[Peanuts|peanuts]], [[Brown|brown]] papery skins removed and discarded\n| 10 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], peeled and crushed\n| 1 to 1.5 teaspoon powdered [[Chile de Arbole|chile de arbole]]\n| 1 teaspoon fine [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| [[Lime]] wedges to garnish\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Heat the [[Oil|oil]] in a [[Frying pan|frying pan]] until hot but not [[Smoking|smoking]]\n| Tip the [[Peanuts|peanuts]] into the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] for 1 minute, keeping them moving all the while\n| Add the [[Garlic|garlic]] and cook for another minute, again, stirring constantly\n| Reduce the heat, add the [[Chilli|chilli]] and [[Salt|salt]] and [[Stir fry|stir fry]] for a further minute\n| Remove from the heat and allow to cool before serving\n}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Garlic recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#peanuts #mexicanchillipeanuts #garlic #chiledearbole #fry #grinding #chilli #mexico #chillipowder #stirfry #lime </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Mexican fishballs in tomato sauce",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mexican fishballs in tomato sauce a fish recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#masaharina #mexicanfishballsintomatosauce #mildmexicanpassata #basa #parsley #whitebread #tabascosauce #egg #fry #whitefish #oliveoil \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Masa harina has such a wonderful unique flavour that it's worth the effort to try and get hold of it\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1487\n|PortionCalories = 743\n|DatePublished=31st October 2012\n|Author=Chef\n|Servings = Serves 2\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes \n |PrepTime = 1 hour 15 minutes\n |CookTime = 15 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mexican fishballs in tomato sauce recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Masa, masa, masa!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Masa Harina is The Boss.  Makes such a difference to this recipe.</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nMasa harina has such a wonderful unique flavour that it's worth the effort to try and get hold of it.  Most [[:Category:Tex-Mex ingredients (supplier)|Mexican ingredient suppliers]] stock it.\n\nMake this with any [[white fish]], [[Basa|basa]] would be my choice as a flavoursome, economical and sustainable fish. Most supermarkets now stock it.\n\n'''fishballs'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 250g [[Basa|basa]] fillets, roughly chopped\n| 1 [[Spring onion|spring onion]], roughly chopped\n| About 200 ml of dried breadcrumbs or 2 slices of [[White bread|white bread]], finely chopped\n| 1 raw [[egg]]\n| A big handful of chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground black pepper|freshly ground black pepper]]\n}}\n'''to coat'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 50g [[Masa harina]]\n}}\n'''for [[Frying|frying]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 tablespoon of butter, 2 tablespoons of [[Olive oil]]\n}}\n''' serve and garnish with'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| [[Tabasco sauce]] or [[Louisiana Hot Pepper Sauce|Louisiana hot pepper sauce]]\n| 1 Sliced [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]]\n| 150 ml [[Sofrito]] or [[Tomato sauce for pizza]]\n| 1 Finely chopped [[Hard-boiled eggs|hard-boiled egg]]\n| 10 [[Olives]]\n| 1 tablespoon freshly chopped [[Parsley|parsley]]\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>>\nImage:Mexican fishballs frying.jpg|thumb|300px|right|Frying the fishballs\nImage:Mexican fishballs in tomato sauce ingredients.jpg|thumb|300px|right|The original ingredients - the recipe has since been slightly modified\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| Add all of the fishball ingredients into a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade and blitz to a rough paste.\n| Roll into small balls and leave to chill in the [[Fridge|fridge]] for an hour or so\n| Add a few tablespoons of [[Masa harina|masa harina]] to a large plate, only a little is needed so don't waste it as I did!\n| Roll the balls in [[Masa harina|masa harina]] to coat.\n| Heat the butter and oil in a large frying pan and shallow [[Fry|fry]] until browned and crispy on the outside\n| Serve with [[Tomato sauce|tomato sauce]] and the garnishes of your choice.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nFor two people this was served with [[Mild Mexican passata]], a portion of pasta for one (100g [[dried pasta]] and a chopped boiled egg.  A very unique and very nice recipe!\n===Variations===\nIf you can get then, fresh [[Poblano chillies|poblano chillies]], [[Roasted|roasted]] and sliced would go well with this as they fairly mild.\n\nI have added a handful of finely chopped [[dried shrimp]] to the mixture.  Not authentic, but adds a nice fishy touch to fishcakes and similar recipes.\n\nWhen I made this I tinkered with the tomato sauce and came up with a separate recipe (if you can call it a recipe), [[Mild Mexican passata]].  It went really well with the fishballs as it had a slightly bitter, chocolatey note.\n===Chef's notes===\nIf you can't get [[Masa harina|masa harina]], coarsely [[Ground|ground]] [[Yellow cornmeal|yellow cornmeal]] would be ok, but it would not have the same distinct flavour.\n\nWhen I made this, the paste was far too wet, so I added another handful of dried breadcrumbs, a little masa, remixed it and set it in a sieve for an hour to drain a little excess liquid.  The result was still quite liquid, but the end result was excellent.  \n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Freshwater fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Sea fish recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#masaharina #mexicanfishballsintomatosauce #mildmexicanpassata #basa #parsley #whitebread #tabascosauce #egg #fry #whitefish #oliveoil </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Mexican meatballs",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Mexican meatballs a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#mexicanmeatballs #courgettes #meatballs #sauce #garlic #eggs #tomatoes #squash #pork #onion #corntortillas \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Surprisingly, this authentic meatball recipe from north western Mexico contains no chillies\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 3076\n|PortionCalories = 512\n|DatePublished=17th January 2013\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = Meatball ingredients, the massive egg turned out to be a double yolker.\n |Servings = Serves 6\n |Difficulty = 2\n |TotalTime = 1 hour 30 minutes\n |PrepTime = 20 minutes\n |CookTime = 1 hour 10 minutes\n |Image = [[Image:Mexican meatballs ingredients.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Gorgeous with spaghetti!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">4.8</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Love the spices in these. I should have been born a Mexican!</span> \n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:PSmith|Paul&nbsp;R&nbsp;Smith]] </span></span>\n}}\nSurprisingly, this authentic meatball recipe from north western Mexico contains no chillies&sect;.  A Chilli sauce such as [[Salsa de chile a la Jalapa]] should of course accompany this dish!\n\nThe trick to these is to slow cook them.\n\n''&sect; [[User:Miguelmartinez|Miguelmartinez]] from San Luis Potos\u00ed, Mexico, suggests adding some [[Jalape\u00f1os|chipotole chillies]] to the mix to make it redder and tastier.''\n\n'''[[Meatballs]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1.5 tablespoons [[Long grain rice|long grain rice]] (white)\n| 340 g (12 oz) [[Minced|minced]] [[Pork|pork]]\n| 340 g (12 oz) [[Minced beef|minced beef]]\n| 180 g [[Courgettes|courgettes]]\n| 2 large [[Eggs|eggs]]\n| &#188; teaspoon [[Mexican oregano]]\n| &#188; teaspoon white [[Cumin seeds|cumin seeds]], crushed\n| 8 [[Peppercorns|peppercorns]], crushed\n| 3 big sprigs of fresh [[Mint|mint]], stalks removed\n| &#190; teaspoons [[Sea Salt|sea salt]]\n| 85 ml finely chopped [[Onion|onion]] (1 small onion)\n}}\n'''[[Sauce]]'''\n{{RecipeIngredientsNB\n| 1 400g can tomatoes\n| 2 tablespoons [[Vegetable oil|vegetable oil]]\n| 250 ml finely chopped [[Onion|onion]] (2 medium onions)\n| 2 [[Fat|fat]] Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]] peeled and crushed\n| 900 ml [[Chicken stock|chicken stock]] or [[Vegetable Stock|vegetable stock]]\n}}\n\n===[[Mise en place]]===\n* Rinse the [[Rice|rice]] under cold running water\n* Cover with [[Boiling|boiling]] water and leave for 45 minutes\n\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Mexican meatballs ready to simmer.jpg|24 meatballs, ready to simmer\nImage:Mexican meatballs with tortillas.jpg|With tortillas and pasta shells!\nImage:Mexican meatballs with spaghetti.jpg|Mexican meatballs with spaghetti\n</gallery>\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| If the [[Pork|pork]] and [[Beef|beef]] is not very finely [[Minced|minced]], blitz for 10 seconds in a [[Food processor|food processor]] with a metal blade for a fine blend\n| Trim the [[Courgettes|courgettes]] or [[Squash|squash]] and chop very finely\n| Add the chopped [[Squash|squash]], the beaten [[Eggs|eggs]] and the remaining [[Meat|meat]]ball ingredients to the [[Meat|meat]] and mix well with your hands until smooth\n| Make 24 [[Meatballs|meatballs]] (about 4 cm diameter)\n| In a large pan, heat the [[Oil|oil]] and [[Fry|fry]] the [[Onions|onions]] and [[Garlic|garlic]] until softened, about 4 minutes.\n| Briefly pulse the tomatoes in a food processor, you don't want a complete puree. Add the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and bring to a [[Boil|boil]], cook and reduce for 4 minutes, stirring often\n| Add the [[Stock|stock]] to the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and once [[Simmering|simmering]], add the [[Meatballs|meatballs]]\n| Cover the pan and [[Simmer|simmer]] for one hour\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe in bowls with plenty of [[Sauce|sauce]], a [[Chili pepper sauce]] and toasted [[corn tortillas]].\n===Chef's notes===\nFor this dish I used [[pork tenderloin fillet]] pulsed to a fine mince in a food processor fitted with a metal blade.  A fattier cut such as shoulder would probably be better in meatballs, but was not available in the quantity I needed.\n\nI made this over two days in two batches.  The first time I added a few pasta shells in the last 10 minutes and served it with lightly fried [[corn tortillas]].  The second time, with [[spaghetti]].   Both were equally good, though I may opt to thicken the sauce a little next time.\n{{Template:ThinkPig}}\n===Variations===\nUse [[Pumpkin|pumpkin]], [[Butternut squash|butternut squash]] etc instead of the [[Courgettes|courgettes]]. I would think squash may need par boiling for 10 minutes first.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Favourite recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#mexicanmeatballs #courgettes #meatballs #sauce #garlic #eggs #tomatoes #squash #pork #onion #corntortillas </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

[[Starters|starters]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 4 medium [[Potatoes|potatoes]]\n| 160g [[Masa harina|masa harina]]\n| 1 small [[Onion|onion]], peeled and [[Grated|grated]]\n| 1 Clove of boiling and peeling.  A dusting of [[yellow cornmeal]] makes them easy to roll and a nice finish.\n\nThe mixture kept well for 4 days, refrigerated in a Lock&Lock box and made really nice sized nibbles by rolling into balls (golf-ball sized), pressing in a [[tortilla-press]] then [[shallow-frying]].\n\nIf you don't have a [[tortilla press]], use 2 chopping boards or just two sheets of wood as a substitute. For this I added half an [[Orange|orange]], sliced; some chopped [[Onion|onion]], muscavado [[Sugar|sugar]] and some [[White wine|white wine]].\n\nI hope Adrienne and Martin enjoy it as much as we did!\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 500g [[Pork shoulder|pork shoulder]]\n| 2 tablespoons [[Taste Sensation Mexican seasoning]]\n| 1 large [[Red onion|red onion]], chopped\n| Half a large [[Orange|orange]], sliced with the rind left on\n| 300 ml [[White wine|white wine]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[Muscovado sugar|muscovado sugar]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Remove any string and excess [[Fat|fat]] or rind from the [[Pork|pork]]\n| Coat both sides of the [[Pork|pork]] with the Taste Sensation [[Mexican]] seasoning\n| Line the [[Slow Cooker|slow cooker]] with the chopped [[Onions|onions]] and half of the [[Orange|orange]] slices\n| Lay the [[Pork|pork]] on to and cover with the remaining [[Orange|orange]] slices\n| Pour the [[White wine|white wine]] into the base of the [[Slow Cooker|slow cooker]]\n| Slow cook on medium for eight hours or so\n| Check halfway through to ensure it is not [[Drying|drying]] out and add a little extra liquid if needed.\n| Remove the rind and drain and excess [[Fat|fat]] with a [[Paper towel|paper towel]]\n| Shred the [[Pork|pork]] into the [[Gravy|gravy]] and serve!\n}}\n\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Pork recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooker recipes]]\n[[Category:Slow cooked]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#orange #pork #whitewine #mexicanpulledpork #porkshoulder #slowcooker #fat #tastesensationrecipes #muscovadosugar #gravy #redonion </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

It works with [[chicken]] as well as [[beef]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 1 packet of [[corn flour tortillas]] or [[wheat flour tortillas]]\n| 225 g (1/2 lb) lean minced [[beef]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[ghee]]\n| Four [[spring onions]], [[chopped on the diagonal]]\n| 1 tablespoon [[tomato puree]]\n| 1 [[red bell pepper]], chopped finely\n| Juice from half an [[orange]]\n}}\n\n'''to garnish'''\n* 150 ml [[Sour cream]]\n* A few tablespoons of grated [[Cheddar]] \n\n====For the spices, use either:====\n\n'''burrito spice mix'''\n* 1 teaspoon dried smoked [[chillies]] such as [[chipotle]]: the smoked [[jalapeno pepper]]\n* 1/4 of a teaspoon of [[black peppercorns]]\n* 5 cm (1/2\") [[cinnamon stick]]\n* 1 teaspoon [[white cumin]] seeds\n* 1 teaspoon [[black cumin]] seeds\n* 1/2 a teaspoon of [[dried minced garlic]]\n* &#189; teaspoon [[dried]] [[oregano]]\n* Good pinch of [[salt]] or 1 tablespoon of juice from [[preserved lemons]]\n\n'''or'''\n* 3 tablespoons of [[Taco mix|Home made taco grinder]]\n| Tip the mince and the [[chopped red peppers]] into a bowl\n| Add the dry [[spices]] and mix them together by kneading the mince\n| Leave for 1 hour or more in a cool place for the flavours to mingle\n| Heat the [[ghee]] in a [[frying]] pan or [[wok]]\n| Add the mince and [[fry]]  until done to your liking\n| Pour off any excess [[fat]]\n| Add the juice from half an [[orange]], the [[tomato pur\u00e9e]] and the chopped [[spring onions]]\n| Stir fry for a few more minutes and pour away any excess liquid\n| Warm the [[tortillas]] (microwave for 15 secs, grill or barbecue or dry fry in a large frying pan )\n| Fill the [[tortillas]] with the minced beef and either roll them or fold them into an envelope\n| Optionally, sprinkle with grated cheese and grill until it bubbles\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe with any or all of the following: [[sour cream]], [[guacamole]], [[pickled jalape\u00f1os]], a  green salad, [[grapefruit salsa]], chopped tomatoes.\n\n===Variations===\n\nTry [[chicken]] fillets or [[shredded]] [[beef]] steak\n\nSlice up a handful of mixed mushrooms, fry them first, discarding any liquid, then add them to the mince.\n{{Tortillas-See also}}\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Beef]]\n[[Category:Main [[Simmer]] gently for 2-3 minutes and season to taste with [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]].\n}}\n<gallery widths=300px heights=300px perrow=5>\nImage:Taste Sensation Nacho Cheese seasoning.jpg|[https://tastesensationltd.com/product/nacho-cheese-seasoning tastesensationltd.com/product/nacho-cheese-seasoning]\nImage:My Taste Sensation Nacho Cheese seasoning.jpg|My packet of nacho seasoning\n</gallery>\n\n===Serving suggestions===\nLovely over [[Boiled potatoes|boiled potatoes]] and cooked [[Green vegetables|green vegetables]] like [[Broccoli|broccoli]]\n===Recipe source===\n\n* [[Taste Sensation Ltd]]\n* https://tastesensationltd.com/product/nacho-cheese-seasoning\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:Dips and sauces]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes]]\n[[Category:Starters]]\n[[Category:Tapas, mezze and antipasti]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes]]\n[[Category:Cheese recipes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Student recipes]]\n[[Category:Taste Sensation recipes]]\n[[Category:Boiled or simmered]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:12032020'>#blend #nacho #nachocheesesaucerecipe #butter #simmer #cheesesauce #boiledorsimmered #recipesfromothersites #boil #salted #starters</code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Nacho chicken salad",
                "revisions": [
                    {

                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Nacho chicken salad; a  recipe\n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#salad #tomatoes #roast #oliveoil #redwinevinegar #coriander #chicken #chives #zest #redonion #lime \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Take your Sunday leftovers to mexico with this quick and easy salad. \n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 1595\n|PortionCalories = 797\n|DatePublished=17th May 2014\n|Author=Chef\n|ImageComment = \n|Servings = Serves 2\n|Difficulty = 1\n|TotalTime =  20 minutes\n|PrepTime =  20 minutes\n|CookTime = None\n|Image = [[Image:Nacho chicken salad recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\">\n<span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">I love Nachos</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5 </span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">Even better when they're served with spicy chicken!</span>\n \n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:TheJudge|The Judge]] </span></span>\n}}\nTake your Sunday leftovers to [[Mexico]] with this quick and easy [[Salad|salad]].\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n\n| 6 large [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] or 500g [[Cherry tomatoes|cherry tomatoes]]\n| 1 [[Red onion|red onion]]\n| A few glugs of [[Olive oil|olive oil]]\n| A handful fresh [[Coriander|coriander]], finely chopped\n| [[Sea Salt|sea salt]] and [[Freshly ground pepper|freshly ground pepper]]\n| 1 teaspoon [[Caster Sugar|caster sugar]], plus an extra pinch\n| 100g cr\u00e8me fra\u00eeche\n| 4 tablespoons finely chopped [[Chives|chives]], plus a pinch to garnish\n| 1 head of [[Lettuce|lettuce]], [[Shredded|shredded]]\n| 2 [[Red peppers|red peppers]]\n| 1 [[Avocado|avocado]], sliced and peeled\n| A few slices or shreds of leftover [[Roast|roast]] [[Chicken|chicken]] *''see variations, below''\n| 2 [[Limes|limes]]\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Red wine vinegar|red wine vinegar]]\n| 2 handfuls of [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]]\n}}\n\n===Method===\n{{RecipeMethod\n\n| Finely [[Dice|dice]] half of your [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] and \u00bd of your [[Red onion|red onion]] to make a little [[Salsa|salsa]]. Mix in a bowl with a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. Finely chop half of your [[Coriander|coriander]]. Stir through. Taste. Mix in a pinch of [[Sugar|sugar]], if needed.\n| In a separate dish, mix your cr\u00e8me fra\u00eeche and [[Chives|chives]]. Season to taste. Garnish with any spare [[Chives|chives]].\n| Heat a clean, [[Dry frying|dry frying]] pan. Add your [[Peppers|peppers]] on a high heat. Turn them every min or so for five mins or till charred. Use tongs to hold the [[Pepper|pepper]], slice into rings. (''see [[Roasted red peppers|roasted red peppers]]'')\n| Finely shred your [[Lettuce|lettuce]] onto a plate.\n| Cut remaining [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] in [[Wedges|wedges]] or halves (if using [[Cherry|cherry]] toms). Thinly slice your [[Onion|onion]], pop in a [[Sieve|sieve]] and pour [[Boiling|boiling]] water over to soften it.Scatter the [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]], [[Onions|onions]], charred [[Pepper|pepper]] slices and [[Avocado|avocado]] over your leaves. Gently mix. Top with slices of cold [[Roast|roast]] [[Chicken|chicken]] and the remaining [[Coriander|coriander]]. \n| Mix the [[Juice|juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of one of your [[Limes|limes]] in a little bowl or [[Jam|jam]] jar with the [[Red wine vinegar|red wine vinegar]], 2 tablespoons [[Olive oil|olive oil]], 1 teaspoon [[Sugar|sugar]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] and [[Pepper|pepper]]. Whisk. Drizzle over your [[Salad|salad]].\n| Cut your [[Lime|lime]] into [[Wedges|wedges]]. Serve alongside the [[Salad|salad]] with the [[Salsa|salsa]], creamy [[Chive dip|chive dip]] and a handful of [[Tortilla chips|tortilla chips]]. Crush another handful of [[Chips|chips]] over your [[Salad|salad]] like [[Croutons|croutons]].\n| For a simple dressing mix the [[Juice|juice]] and [[Zest|zest]] of 1 [[Lime|lime]] with the [[Sugar|sugar]], [[Red wine vinegar|red wine vinegar]] and [[Olive oil|olive oil]]. Drizzle over the [[Salad|salad]].\n}}\n===Variations===\nNo leftover [[Roast|roast]] [[Chicken|chicken]]? [[Roast]] [[Chicken thighs|chicken thighs]] in a 220\u00b0C/Gas 7 [[Oven|oven]] for 35 mins, or till golden, crispy-skinned and cooked through.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:British recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Salad recipes]]\n[[Category:Abel and Cole veg box recipes]]\n[[Category:Uncooked]]\n{{Template:Abel and Cole veg box recipes attribution}}\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n[[Category:Recipes from other sites]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#salad #tomatoes #roast #oliveoil #redwinevinegar #coriander #chicken #chives #zest #redonion #lime </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }

Do not allow them to burn.\n| Lower heat and add the [[Garlic|garlic]], again, stirring all the time.\n| When the [[Garlic|garlic]] is golden, stir in  the [[Chipotle|chipotle]] paste and add the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n| Turn off the heat, but leave on the hob, shaking the pan until the [[Seeds|seeds]] are coated with the [[Sugar|sugar]].\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\nServe with the [[Lime|lime]] half, the [[Juice|juice]] of which should be squeezed over the [[Seeds|seeds]].\n===Variations===\n[[Chipotle]] paste is available from Waitrose, but if you cannot get it, use 2 teaspoons [[Dried|dried]] [[Chilli flakes|chilli flakes]] and a pinch of [[Salt|salt]] instead.\n===Chef's notes===\nThe [[Seeds|seeds]] will stay fairly fresh if you store them in a [[Lock&Lock boxes|Lock&Lock box]], but do not add the [[Lime|lime]] until they are served.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Chilli pepper recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Snacks and light bites|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Spicy recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Vegetarian recipes|Pepitas picantes]]\n[[Category:Vegan recipes]]\n[[Category:Squash recipes]]\n[[Category:Dry fried]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#pepitaspicantes #pumpkinseeds #lime #garlic #chipotle #seeds #chilli #toasted #dried #chilliflakes #unusualrecipes </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"

title": "Picadillo",
                "revisions": [
                    {
                        "contentformat": "text/x-wiki",
                        "contentmodel": "wikitext",
                        "*": "<!-- seo -->\n{{#seo:\n|title=Picadillo a beef recipe \n|titlemode=replace\n|keywords=#picadillo #beef #bellpepper #tomatoes #garlic #potato #vegetables #spanishrice #unusualrecipes #browning #diced \n|hashtagrev=032020\n|description=Picadillo is a dish mainly consisting of ground beef typically found in Puerto Rico, Cuba, Mexico, and other Latin American countries\n}}\n<!-- /seo -->\n\n{{Template:CookTools}}\n{{recipesummary\n|TotalCalories = 2856\n|PortionCalories = 476\n|DatePublished=8th December 2013\n|Author=JuliaBalbilla\n|Servings = Serves 6\n|Difficulty = 2\n|TotalTime = 50 minutes\n|PrepTime = 10 minutes\n|CookTime = 40 minutes\n|Image = [[Image:Picadillo recipe.jpg|alt=Electus]]\n<span class=\"review\"> <span class=\"reviewHeader\">\n====Best recipe review====\n</span>\n''<span class=\"reviewTitle\">Home cooking!</span>''\n\n<span style=\"line-height:180%\"><span style=\"font-size:180%;\"><span class=\"reviewScore\">5</span>/5</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewDesc\">We love this</span>\n\n<span class=\"reviewAuthor\"> [[User:Carla_Cancio-Bello,_J.D.,_on_behalf_of_Cuban_Cuisine_UK|Carla]] </span></span>\n}}\n\nPicadillo is a dish mainly consisting of ground [[Beef|beef]] typically found in Puerto Rico, Cuba, Mexico, and other Latin American countries. In Mexico and Puerto Rico it is sometimes used as a filling, such as for [[Tacos|tacos]], and can be mixed with [[Vegetables|vegetables]]. It can also be prepared as a type of stew. In most other Latin American countries it consists of a common table from where people pick small beef pieces or other food such as [[French fries|french fries]]. The name comes from the Spanish word, \"picar\" which means \"to mince\" or \"to chop\".\n\n{{RecipeIngredients\n| 500 g (1 lb 2 oz) of lean [[minced]] [[Beef|beef]]\n| 1 large [[Onion|onion]], peeled and chopped\n| 4 Cloves of [[Garlic|garlic]], chopped\n| 284 ml (&frac12; pint) [[Beef stock|beef stock]] \n| 1 large [[Green bell pepper|green bell pepper]],deseeded and chopped\n| 3 large russet [[Potato|potato]], cubed, bite size\n| 1 400 g (14.5 oz) tin [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]] together with the juice\n| 2 tablespoons of [[Oil|oil]]\n| 1/8 teaspoon [[Sea salt|sea salt]] \n| 2 tablespoons of [[Tex-Mex seasoning]]\n}}\n===Method===\n\n{{RecipeMethod\n| In a large, heavy pan, heat the [[Oil|oil]] to medium-high heat. Add the [[Onions|onions]], [[Garlic|garlic]], [[Bell pepper|bell pepper]] and seasoning to the pan.\n| When the [[Bell pepper|bell pepper]] starts to discolour, add to it ground [[Beef|beef]], stirring to break up large pieces and [[Brown|brown]] evenly, about 7 minutes. \n| As [[Meat|meat]] is [[Browning|browning]], add [[Potato|potato]], [[Beef|beef]] broth and [[Diced|diced]] [[Tomatoes|tomatoes]]. \n| [[Simmer]] until the potato is cooked and the picadillo has thickened, stirring occasionally.\n}}\n===Serving suggestions===\n\nServe hot with [[Spanish rice]] and tortilla.\n{{RecipeLine}}\n[[Category:Recipes]]\n[[Category:Beef recipes]]\n[[Category:Latin American recipes]]\n[[Category:Main courses]]\n[[Category:Meat recipes]]\n[[Category:Mexican recipes]]\n[[Category:Tex-Mex recipes]]\n[[Category:North American recipes]]\n[[Category:Pan fried]]\n[[Category:Cuban recipes]]\n[[Category:Unusual recipes]]\n\n<!-- footer hashtags --><code 'hashtagrev:032020'>#picadillo #beef #bellpepper #tomatoes #garlic #potato #vegetables #spanishrice #unusualrecipes #browning #diced </code><!-- /footer_hashtags -->"
                    }
                ]
            }
        }
    }
